# 雀魂

<body>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">雀魂</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">本质：特异本质</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">总描述：在某个麻将为全民娱乐的世界下，有着这么一间神秘的魂天神社，各路人士，甚至妖怪，神明都齐聚一堂，只为了打麻将。这些麻将水准相比一般人更高的人，我们将其称为雀士。而雀士的麻将，并不仅仅只是麻将，还蕴含着其他的力量。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">============================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体"> </font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">兑换提示：本称号其实是一个纯粹的数值称号，其触发非常不稳定，因为你无法确定自己和什么牌。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">所有的特性都是基于和牌来进行计算，</font>C级和B级的手牌是某种意义上的保险。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">其和牌的特性非常强力，但是也非常不稳定，所以常见的方法是想法设法是组织一套牌，然后到</font>BOSS战的时候进行和牌，从而获得强力效果。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">还有就是本称号带来的幸运加值与修行加值无法叠加，所以习得其他修炼体系或者称号的时候需要注意。</font></span><!--EndFragment--></p></font></span></font></span>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">============================================================================================================</font></span></font></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特殊：当你获得本称号时，你将获得一个【牌山】计量池，如同真正的日麻一样，其具有数牌（即为从一到九的万子、条子、筒子），以及字牌（即东南西北中白发）组成，本称号的【牌山】中的牌以一百零八张为一套，彻底消耗完毕这一百零八张之后自动获得新的一套，所以总量是无限的。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">当你离开剧情世界时，你保留上一个世界最后的手牌和其强化效果，当你进入下一个剧情世界时，你失去之前的手牌和强化效果，在刷新牌山</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">（洗牌）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">至一百零八张满后，从中随机获得</font>13张手牌。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">你可以使用骰子确认手牌</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">的牌面</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">，投掷一个</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">1D4</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">，按照万条筒</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">字</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">的顺序决定种类，若为万、条、筒，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">字（东西南北中发白）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">则再投掷一个</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">D</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">9确认具体的数字</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">和字（</font>1D7）</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">。（当然最方便的是打开雀魂开一把），一个牌（例如一条、三万、八筒、东风）在一个牌山中最多有四张，若在没有切换牌山时获得同种牌的第五张，则该张牌重新抽取。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">将手牌记录下来后，将其作为你的初始手牌。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">随后，你每天可以进行一次摸牌和切牌，摸牌就是再按照确认手牌的方式，再获得一张牌，切牌就是将一张牌打出，打出的牌视为消失而非回到牌山。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">你摸牌后的手牌不能超过上限。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">宝牌：宝牌是一种普通牌，其在组成牌型的时候按照普通牌的牌面进行判断，只有特殊的情况下，宝牌才有特殊效果。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特殊规则：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">立直：将立直棒打出，宣告立直，之后无论你摸到什么牌都必须打出去，直到和牌为止。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">当你的手牌只差一张就能和牌时，你可以选择这</font>13张手牌宣告立直（若你第一次摸牌之后就出现这种情况，则可以进行双立直），在这之后，你无法再更换这13张手牌，并且“小林立都不敢这么画”效果对这13张手牌不起效，无法通过指定摸牌来令其达成和牌。（立直会影响你和牌后的番数）</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">============================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体"> </font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">等级</font>D 初心</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font>D+1000</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能量池：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">技能树：开启</font>D级技能树</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特性：和牌（四特性）、幸运</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特殊：由于没有能量池，额外获得</font>1个特性。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：刚开始接触麻将的你，还什么都不会呢，哪里亮了点哪里，想要获胜恐怕只能依靠运气了吧。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; DISPLAY: none; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-hide: all"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; DISPLAY: none; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-hide: all"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: middle; WORD-BREAK: break-all; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">和牌：麻将一共</font>13张手牌。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: middle; WORD-BREAK: break-all; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">13张手牌+摸的一张牌一共14张，需要满足4个组合和1个对子。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: middle; WORD-BREAK: break-all; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">4个组合可以是顺子，刻子，和杠（杠是4张，但是可以额外摸一张，所以手牌总数不变）。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: middle; WORD-BREAK: break-all; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">当完成</font>4个组合+1个对子的牌型之后，即为“和牌“也就是”门前请“。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: middle; WORD-BREAK: break-all; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">然后根据其组合的情况按照下表对照，计算番或者倍数，获得总分。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: middle; WORD-BREAK: break-all; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特殊：当你和牌的时候，手中有宝牌，则每张宝牌算做一番。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: middle; WORD-BREAK: break-all; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: middle; WORD-BREAK: break-all; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">小牌面：按照和牌的牌型计算番数，满足多个牌型番数可以叠加，计算最终的番数后，根据最后的</font>“点数速查表”来确定分数。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: middle; WORD-BREAK: break-all; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: middle; WORD-BREAK: break-all; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">所有数牌均为同一花色，没有字牌。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p></td>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: middle; WORD-BREAK: break-all; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: middle; WORD-BREAK: break-all; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">大牌面：计算最终的分数为</font>48000乘以倍数。如一倍就是乘以1，两倍就是乘以2.</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: middle; WORD-BREAK: break-all; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">大牌面与小牌面不叠加计算。当和牌的时候既满足大牌面的组合和小牌面的组合时，只计算大牌面。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: middle; WORD-BREAK: break-all; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">同时，大牌面之间可以互相叠加，如满足</font>“天和”和“国士无双”，则变成两倍。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; PADDING-RIGHT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">当你凑出和牌的牌型时，你可以随时宣布和牌！计算和牌的分数，然后分数除以</font>1000，得到X，向下取整。如一番，最终的X就是1，然后你可以根据自己的意愿分配X到你的单项检定获得分配的幸运加值。（如你可以指定咆哮检定获得1DP幸运加值，但是你无法指定胁迫相关检定获得1DP幸运加值，近战攻击，远程攻击，防御，施法，心灵，三豁免（分别指定）检定，先攻（这会改变先攻顺序）。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特殊的是，本能力带来的幸运加值无法与修行加值叠加。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特殊的是，若一次检定同时满足两种情况，比如施法进行远程攻击检定，则只能计算一次本加值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这些加值能够持续一天，这被称之为和牌状态下，同时根据不同的和牌牌型还可以获得特殊效果（这会出现在你的技能树中）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">和牌状态结束后（也就是第二天），你将重新开始打牌。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">若你有任何能力让你重新开始打牌，则和牌状态也会立即结束。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特殊的是：你最大为一个检定分配的加值为你的传奇风度</font>+1/点。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">幸运：你的机运骰结果</font>+1。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">============================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体"> </font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">等级</font>C 雀圣</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font>C+2000</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">技能树：开启</font>C级雀魂技能树</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特性：宝牌（双特性），</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">手牌（双特性）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：你太神仙了，以至于你直接跳过雀杰和雀豪，来到了雀圣的段位。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">宝牌：你每天有一次机会可以进行一次机运检定，如果成功，则可以将手牌中的一张牌变</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">指定为</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">宝牌</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">（这不会影响该牌原本的牌面）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">，宝牌是一种奖励牌，仅在有本级效果时，宝牌没有任何作用。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">手牌：你的手牌中每有两张万子，你就可以在攻击检定上获得</font>1DP幸运加值。你的手牌中每有两张条子，你就能在防御上获得1点幸运加值。你的手牌中每有两张筒子，你就可以在施法以及心灵检定上获得1DP幸运加值。你的手牌中每有两张字牌，则你的先攻检定增加1点。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特殊：若是一个施法检定或者心灵检定进行的攻击，则只能获得一次加值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">============================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体"> </font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">等级</font>B 魂天</span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font>B+4000</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">技能树：开启</font>B级雀魂技能树</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特性：小林立都不敢这么画，杠！</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">手牌（提升特性），</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">真正的超能力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">（双特性）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：魂</font>天段位，此即为雀士中对最强者的称呼。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">小林立都不敢这么画：你打的简直是超能力麻将，无论什么牌都可以被你摸到。现在的你，每天进行摸切的时候，可以消耗</font>1点意志力，从当前剩余牌山中指定一张牌将其摸出，这会正常的占用你每天的摸牌数量。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">杠！：当你手牌中有四张完全一样的牌时，你可以将其组成一个杠，同时立即再摸一张牌。</font></span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">手牌：现在你的手牌中每有一个顺子（数牌的一种特殊套装型，顺子必须是连着的三个相同花色并且连续的数字牌组成的。）或刻子（刻子就是同样牌的三张组成的特殊套装型，可以是数牌也可以是字牌，刻子必须是同样的三张牌组成的。），就可以将提供的对应加值额外再加</font>3点。已经参与了顺子和刻子计算的手牌，无法再进行其他顺子、刻子的计算。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">真正的超能力：超能力麻将根本不需要乖乖摸切。当你进入</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">冒险</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">世界后，若你对于你的初始手牌不满意，则你可以将不超过你传奇风度</font>/张的手牌重新摸牌。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">============================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">雀魂</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">D级</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">技能树</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：拔北，指的是三人麻将中，将北作为宝牌打出，并再次摸一张牌的操作。即使打出了拔北宝牌，也会算一张宝牌，算做一番。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：当你的手牌中有字牌北（或称北风）时，你可以消耗</font>1点意志力，将该张北牌</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">移除牌山（也就是牌山永久减少</font>1张北牌，除非重新洗牌），然后重新摸一张牌，正在计算牌面。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">同时，在计算宝牌数量时，增加</font>1张。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续至下一次洗牌为止。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">============================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">  
 </font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font>D+500</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：标准动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能耗：</font>1点意志力</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">风度值</font>/米</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：一个目标</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：见下</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：由于本称号是一人麻将，所以不存在鸣牌的情况，若是想要达成暗刻，就必须要购买本技能。所谓暗刻即为不通过碰别人的牌，仅靠自己摸牌达成的刻子。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：当你的手中持有一个刻子时，你可以宣告这个刻子是一个暗刻，然后该刻子带来的加值变为减值，接着你可以选定你敏感范围内的一个目标，令其来承受这个减值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">若其施展的法术（或者能力）原本支线等级在</font>C级以下则直接被打断，其使用的材料，能耗，动作等全部被消耗，该效果直接结束（如对方进行一次攻击，则该次攻击直接失败）。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">若其施展的法术（或者能力）原本的支线等级超过</font>C级，则你进行施法检定，目标以该能力的施展检定进行对抗（主属性与主技能，施法检定，心灵检定），若你失败，则其可以正常施展，否则其被打断。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">对方施展的法术（或者能力）原本的支线等级若比你高</font>1级，则其检定获得3点附加成功，若你比高2级，则其检定获得9点附加成功，若比你高3级，则其检定获得27点附加成功。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：当你的手牌可以和牌时，你可以将手牌中的一张牌交给目标，并令其在下一回合开始时打出。由于【牌山】只有你才能看见，这个过程对方是无法看见的，同时也无关对方的意愿，到达时点后目标一定会打出这张牌（哪怕对方也拥有雀魂称号也会打出这张牌）。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：大三元为较为常见的役满牌型，和牌时，手牌中含有中白发组成的刻子即可。大三元在古时为科举制度名词，同省乡试解元、全国会试会元、殿试状元合称大三元，为中国古代科举制度下的读书人最高成就。在浩如烟海的中国古代科举历史中，大三元及第的文臣仅有</font>14人。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：当你以大三元的牌型和牌时，你可以选择一个目标，该目标与你一同获得大三元的幸运加值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：九莲宝灯是最难达成的役满，要求在和牌时，手牌中只包含同种花色的</font>1112345678999，再加以上任意一张。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：当你以</font>“九莲宝灯”或者“</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">纯正九莲宝灯</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(51,51,51); FONT-STYLE: normal; LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">”</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">的牌型和牌时，在其和牌状态期间内，自动获得本效果：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">你获得</font>9盏美丽的莲花宝灯围绕着你飞舞，每盏莲花宝灯都可以抵挡一次致命伤害。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">当你将要因为受到一次伤害而死亡时</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">，</font>9盏莲花宝灯将为你挡下该伤害，你免疫该次伤害。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">注意，不可避免的伤害无法通过本能力免疫。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman'; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">注意，即死效果或者不通过造成伤害杀死你的能力，本技能无能无力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman'; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
